## Analysis

The GT expression is:
$$0.3156 \cdot P \cdot e^{-0.05405t} + \frac{0.3156 \cdot P^2}{9.8709P + 1}$$

Let me check the candidates systematically.

**Candidate 31**: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3/(P + c4)`

This gives: $c_0 P e^{c_1 t} + c_2 P + \frac{c_3 P}{P + c_4}$

The GT's second term is $\frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709P + 1}$. We can rewrite this as $\frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709(P + 1/9.8709)} = \frac{(0.3156/9.8709) P^2}{P + 0.10131}$.

But candidate 31 has $\frac{c_3 P}{P + c_4}$, not $\frac{c_3 P^2}{P + c_4}$. These are structurally different. So candidate 31 doesn't match unless we can absorb the extra P elsewhere, but there's no standalone $P^2/(P+c)$ term. Setting $c_2 = 0$ doesn't help either.

**Candidate 30**: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3/(P*c4 + c5) + c6/(P*c4 + c5)`

This gives: $c_0 P e^{c_1 t} + c_2 P + \frac{c_3 P}{c_4 P + c_5} + \frac{c_6}{c_4 P + c_5}$

The GT second term: $\frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709P + 1} = \frac{0.3156 P \cdot P}{9.8709P + 1}$. 

In candidate 30, $\frac{c_3 P}{c_4 P + c_5}$ provides $\frac{P}{c_4 P + c_5}$ type terms, not $\frac{P^2}{...}$.

**Candidate 33**: `P**2*c0/(P + c1) + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4`

This gives: $\frac{c_0 P^2}{P + c_1} + c_2 P e^{c_3 t} + c_4 P$

Setting: $c_0 = 0.3156/9.8709 = 0.03197$, $c_1 = 1/9.8709 = 0.10131$... Wait, the GT's second term is $\frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709P + 1}$. We need $\frac{c_0 P^2}{P + c_1} = \frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709P + 1} = \frac{(0.3156/9.8709) P^2}{P + 1/9.8709}$.

So $c_0 = 0.3156/9.8709 \approx 0.03197$, $c_1 = 1/9.8709 \approx 0.10131$.

Then $c_2 = 0.3156$, $c_3 = -0.05405$, $c_4 = 0$.

This gives: $\frac{0.03197 P^2}{P + 0.10131} + 0.3156 P e^{-0.05405t} + 0$

Which equals: $\frac{0.3156 P^2}{9.8709P + 1} + 0.3156 P e^{-0.05405t}$

This matches the GT exactly! ✓

**Candidate 33 matches the GT** with:
- $c_0 = 0.3156/9.8709$
- $c_1 = 1/9.8709$
- $c_2 = 0.3156$
- $c_3 = -0.05405$
- $c_4 = 0$
